# List Calls

**URL:** https://docs.ultravox.ai/api-reference/calls/calls-list

## Description
Returns details for all calls

## Endpoint
```
GET /api/call
```

## Request/Response Examples

data-component-part="field-info-pill"><span>enum&lt;string&gt;</span></div><div class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-red-100/50 dark:bg-red-400/10 text-red-600 dark:text-red-300 font-medium whitespace-nowrap" data-component-part="field-required-pill">required</div></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-4"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal prose prose-sm prose-gray dark:prose-invert overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><ul class="list-inside list-disc whitespace-normal" data-streamdown="unordered-list">
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_PENDING* - The call hasn&#x27;t been billed yet, but will be in the future. This is the case for ongoing calls for example. (Note: Calls created before May 28, 2025 may have this status even if they were billed.)</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_FREE_CONSOLE* - The call was free because it was initiated on <a href="https://app.ultravox.ai" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link" node="[object Object]">https://app.ultravox.ai</a>.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_FREE_ZERO_EFFECTIVE_DURATION* - The call was free because its effective duration was zero. (Note: There may still be a non-zero sip bill in this case.)</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_FREE_MINUTES* - The call was unbilled but counted against the account&#x27;s free minutes. (Note: There may still be a non-zero sip bill in this case.)</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_FREE_SYSTEM_ERROR* - The call was free because it ended due to a system error.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_FREE_OTHER* - The call is in an undocumented free billing state.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_BILLED* - The call was billed. See billedDuration for the billed duration.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_REFUNDED* - The call was billed but was later refunded.</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">BILLING_STATUS_UNSPECIFIED* - The call is in an unexpected billing state. Please contact support.</li>
</ul></div><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap prose-sm mt-6">Available options<!-- -->:<!-- --> <div class="inline-block"><code>BILLING_STATUS_PENDING</code>,<!-- --> </div><div header (thus really returning raw PCM), set this to audio/l16. Similarly, if your API claims to

class="font-semibold text-primary dark:text-primary-light cursor-pointer overflow-wrap-anywhere" data-component-part="field-name"><span class="text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">results.vadSettings.</span>turnEndpointDelay</div><div class="inline items-center gap-2 text-xs font-medium [&amp;_div]:inline [&amp;_div]:mr-2 [&amp;_div]:leading-5" data-component-part="field-meta"><div class="flex items-center px-2 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-gray-100/50 dark:bg-white/5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-200 font-medium break-all" data-component-part="field-info-pill"><span>string</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-4"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal prose prose-sm prose-gray dark:prose-invert overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><p class="whitespace-pre-line">The minimum amount of time the agent will wait to respond after the user seems to be done
speaking. Increasing this value will make the agent less eager to respond, which may increase
perceived response latency but will also make the agent less likely to jump in before the user
is really done speaking.</p>
<p class="whitespace-pre-line">Built-in VAD currently operates on 32ms frames, so only multiples of 32ms are meaningful.
(Anything from 1ms to 31ms will produce the same result.)</p>
<p class="whitespace-pre-line">Defaults to &quot;0.384s&quot; (384ms) as a starting point, but there&#x27;s nothing special about this value
aside from it corresponding to 12 VAD frames.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="primitive-param-field border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-b last:border-b-0"><div class="py-6"><div class="flex font-mono text-sm group/param-head param-head break-all relative" id="response-results-items-vad-settings-minimum-turn-duration"><div class="flex-1 flex flex-col content-start py-0.5 mr-5"><div class="flex items-center flex-wrap gap-2"><div class="absolute -top-1.5"><a href="#response-results-items-vad-settings-minimum-turn-duration" class="-ml-[2.1rem] flex items-center opacity-0 dark:text-gray-400">results.vadSettings.</span>minimumTurnDuration</div><div class="inline items-center gap-2 text-xs font-medium [&amp;_div]:inline [&amp;_div]:mr-2 [&amp;_div]:leading-5" data-component-part="field-meta"><div class="flex items-center px-2 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-gray-100/50 dark:bg-white/5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-200 font-medium break-all" data-component-part="field-info-pill"><span>string</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-4"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal prose prose-sm prose-gray dark:prose-invert overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><p class="whitespace-pre-line">The minimum duration of user speech required to be considered a user turn.
Increasing this value will cause the agent to ignore short user audio. This may be useful in
particularly noisy environments, but it comes at the cost of possibly ignoring very short
user responses such as &quot;yes&quot; or &quot;no&quot;.</p>
<p class="whitespace-pre-line">Defaults to &quot;0s&quot; meaning the agent considers all user audio inputs (that make it through
built-in noise cancellation).</p></div></div></div></div><div class="primitive-param-field border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-b last:border-b-0"><div class="py-6"><div class="flex font-mono
